**inline**   vim\EQUATION_EXTRACTION_SUPPLEMENT.md
```latex
\(\frac{d\mathbf{x}}{dt} = -\nabla_{\mathbf{x}} V(\mathbf{x}) + \mathcal{D}(D(t)) + \mathcal{K}(\mathbf{x}) + \mathcal{S}(\mathbf{x}, \mathcal{R}_{24})\)
```

**inline**   vim\EQUATION_EXTRACTION_SUPPLEMENT.md
```latex
\(V = (\beta - 1)^2\)
```

**inline**   vim\EQUATION_EXTRACTION_SUPPLEMENT.md
```latex
\(\nabla V = 2(\beta - 1)\nabla \beta\)
```

**inline**   vim\EQUATION_EXTRACTION_SUPPLEMENT.md
```latex
\(F_{\text{restore}} = -2(\beta - 1)\nabla \beta\)
```

**inline**   vim\EQUATION_EXTRACTION_SUPPLEMENT.md
```latex
\(\mathcal{D}(D(t)) = \sigma \cdot D(t) \cdot \mathbf{u}_{\text{harm}}\)
```

**inline**   vim\EQUATION_EXTRACTION_SUPPLEMENT.md
```latex
\(D(t) \in \mathbb{R}^{+}\)
```

**inline**   vim\EQUATION_EXTRACTION_SUPPLEMENT.md
```latex
\(\mathcal{K} = \mathbf{M}_{\text{struct}} \cdot \mathbf{x} + \mathbf{M}_{\text{harm}} \cdot \mathbf{x}\)
```

**inline**   vim\EQUATION_EXTRACTION_SUPPLEMENT.md
```latex
\(\mathcal{S} = \mathbf{R}_{24}(\mathbf{x}) \cdot \mathbf{x}\)
```

**inline**   vim\EQUATION_EXTRACTION_SUPPLEMENT.md
```latex
\(\frac{d\mathbf{x}}{dt} \approx -2(\beta - 1)\nabla \beta\)
```

**inline**   vim\EQUATION_EXTRACTION_SUPPLEMENT.md

## 5. Bibliography

### BibTeX style

Common choices: `plain`, `unsrt`, `alpha`, `apalike`.

```latex
\bibliographystyle{plain}
\bibliography{vim_refs}
```

### .bib file structure

```bibtex
@article{edwards2026vim,
  author  = {Edwards, Ross A.},
  title   = {Vacuum Impedance Matching and the Theory of Balan…
```

**display**   vim\section_c.md
```latex
\[
\delta \mathcal{S}_{\text{Unified}} = 0
\quad \Longleftrightarrow \quad
\delta \Gamma_{\text{bdy}} = 0
\quad \Longleftrightarrow \quad
\delta \mathcal{D}_{\text{coh}} = 0
\quad \Longleftrightarrow \quad
\delta S_{\text{ent}} = 0.
\]
```

**inline**   vim\section_c.md
```latex
\(g_{ab}\)
```

**inline**   vim\section_c.md
```latex
\(\mathcal{I}_{ab}\)
```

**display**   vim\section_c.md
```latex
\[
\mathcal{G}_{ab}
=
g_{ab}
+ \lambda_{\mathcal{I}} \mathcal{I}_{ab}
+ \lambda_{\Phi} \nabla_a \Phi_{\text{HIF}} \nabla_b \Phi_{\text{HIF}}.
\]
```

```latex
\]
```
